Page name: File:Network wide ban.png
Edit type: upload
Url: http://wiki.scratch.mit.edu/w/images/Network_wide_ban.png
Comment: Transfering images from http://wiki.scratch.mit.edu/w
Text: 
An example of a network wide ban on Scratch 2.0? From school (where the ban is), I can still access the website, but cannot participate in the community. When attempting to post a comment, forum post, or edit a text field on a project/profile - this message box shows up and the changes are not accepted. At home where I'm on a different network, I can use Scratch normally from the same account.
